<Tag slot="tag">

<TagTitle slot="title">

# Beta Agents Endpoints

</TagTitle>

<TagDescription slot="description">

(beta) Agents API

</TagDescription>

</Tag>

<Operation>

<OperationTitleSection slot="title">

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>GET</b></Pill> /v1/agents \{#operation-agents_api_v1_agents_list\}

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_List agent entities._

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

Retrieve a list of agent entities sorted by creation time.

</OperationDescriptionSection>

<OperationCodeSamplesSection slot="code-samples">

<TabbedSection>

  slot="tab"

  dependencyUrlPrefix="/try-it-now"
  defaultValue="import { Mistral } from &quot;@mistralai/mistralai&quot;;&NewLine;&NewLine;const mistral = new Mistral({&NewLine;  apiKey: &quot;MISTRAL_API_KEY&quot;,&NewLine;});&NewLine;&NewLine;async function run() {&NewLine;  const result = await mistral.beta.agents.list({});&NewLine;&NewLine;  console.log(result);&NewLine;}&NewLine;&NewLine;run();&NewLine;"
  packageName="@mistralai/mistralai"

<SectionTab
  slot="tab"
  id="operation-agents_api_v1_agents_list+code-samples+python"
  tags={{"codeSample":"python"}}
>

Python

</SectionTab>

<SectionContent slot="content" id="operation-agents_api_v1_agents_list+code-samples+python">

<CodeSample>

```python
from mistralai import Mistral
import os


with Mistral(
    api_key=os.getenv("MISTRAL_API_KEY", ""),
) as mistral:

    res = mistral.beta.agents.list(page=0, page_size=20)

    # Handle response
    print(res)


```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### type \{#operation-agents_api_v1_agents_list+responses+200+application-json+agent+completion_args+completionargs+response_format+responseformat+type\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

An object specifying the format that the model must output. Setting to `\{ "type": "json_object" \}` enables JSON mode, which guarantees the message the model generates is in JSON. When using JSON mode you MUST also instruct the model to produce JSON yourself with a system or a user message.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

<Operation>

<OperationTitleSection slot="title">

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>POST</b></Pill> /v1/agents \{#operation-agents_api_v1_agents_create\}

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_Create a agent that can be used within a conversation._

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

Create a new agent giving it instructions, tools, description. The agent is then available to be used as a regular assistant in a conversation or as part of an agent pool from which it can be used.

</OperationDescriptionSection>

<OperationCodeSamplesSection slot="code-samples">

<TabbedSection>

<SectionTab
  slot="tab"
  id="operation-agents_api_v1_agents_create+code-samples+typescript"
  tags={{"codeSample":"typescript"}}
>

TypeScript

</SectionTab>

<SectionContent
  slot="content"
  id="operation-agents_api_v1_agents_create+code-samples+typescript"

  defaultValue="import { Mistral } from &quot;@mistralai/mistralai&quot;;&NewLine;&NewLine;const mistral = new Mistral({&NewLine;  apiKey: &quot;MISTRAL_API_KEY&quot;,&NewLine;});&NewLine;&NewLine;async function run() {&NewLine;  const result = await mistral.beta.agents.create({&NewLine;    model: &quot;LeBaron&quot;,&NewLine;    name: &quot;&lt;value&gt;&quot;,&NewLine;  });&NewLine;&NewLine;  console.log(result);&NewLine;}&NewLine;&NewLine;run();&NewLine;"

<SectionTab
  slot="tab"
  id="operation-agents_api_v1_agents_create+code-samples+python"
  tags={{"codeSample":"python"}}
>

Python

</SectionTab>

<SectionContent slot="content" id="operation-agents_api_v1_agents_create+code-samples+python">

<CodeSample>

```python
from mistralai import Mistral
import os


with Mistral(
    api_key=os.getenv("MISTRAL_API_KEY", ""),
) as mistral:

    res = mistral.beta.agents.create(model="LeBaron", name="<value>")

    # Handle response
    print(res)


```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

  slot="tab"

cURL

```curl
curl https://api.mistral.ai/v1/agents \
 -X POST \
 -H 'Authorization: Bearer YOUR_APIKEY_HERE' \
 -d '{
  "model": "ipsum eiusmod",
  "name": "consequat do"
}'
```

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### type \{#operation-agents_api_v1_agents_create+request+completion_args+completionargs+response_format+responseformat+type\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

An object specifying the format that the model must output. Setting to `\{ "type": "json_object" \}` enables JSON mode, which guarantees the message the model generates is in JSON. When using JSON mode you MUST also instruct the model to produce JSON yourself with a system or a user message.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

##### type \{#operation-agents_api_v1_agents_create+responses+200+application-json+completion_args+completionargs+response_format+responseformat+type\}

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

An object specifying the format that the model must output. Setting to `\{ "type": "json_object" \}` enables JSON mode, which guarantees the message the model generates is in JSON. When using JSON mode you MUST also instruct the model to produce JSON yourself with a system or a user message.

<Operation>

<OperationTitleSection slot="title">

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>GET</b></Pill> /v1/agents/\{agent\_id\} \{#operation-agents_api_v1_agents_get\}

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_Retrieve an agent entity._

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

Given an agent retrieve an agent entity with its attributes.

</OperationDescriptionSection>

<OperationCodeSamplesSection slot="code-samples">

Python

<CodeSample>

```python
from mistralai import Mistral
import os


with Mistral(
    api_key=os.getenv("MISTRAL_API_KEY", ""),
) as mistral:

    res = mistral.beta.agents.get(agent_id="<id>")

    # Handle response
    print(res)


```

</CodeSample>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### type \{#operation-agents_api_v1_agents_get+responses+200+application-json+completion_args+completionargs+response_format+responseformat+type\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

An object specifying the format that the model must output. Setting to `\{ "type": "json_object" \}` enables JSON mode, which guarantees the message the model generates is in JSON. When using JSON mode you MUST also instruct the model to produce JSON yourself with a system or a user message.

<OperationTitleSection slot="title">

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>PATCH</b></Pill> /v1/agents/\{agent\_id\} \{#operation-agents_api_v1_agents_update\}

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_Update an agent entity._

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

Update an agent attributes and create a new version.

</OperationDescriptionSection>

<OperationCodeSamplesSection slot="code-samples">

Python

<CodeSample>

```python
from mistralai import Mistral
import os


with Mistral(
    api_key=os.getenv("MISTRAL_API_KEY", ""),
) as mistral:

    res = mistral.beta.agents.update(agent_id="<id>")

    # Handle response
    print(res)


```

</CodeSample>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### type \{#operation-agents_api_v1_agents_update+request+completion_args+completionargs+response_format+responseformat+type\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

An object specifying the format that the model must output. Setting to `\{ "type": "json_object" \}` enables JSON mode, which guarantees the message the model generates is in JSON. When using JSON mode you MUST also instruct the model to produce JSON yourself with a system or a user message.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### type \{#operation-agents_api_v1_agents_update+responses+200+application-json+completion_args+completionargs+response_format+responseformat+type\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

An object specifying the format that the model must output. Setting to `\{ "type": "json_object" \}` enables JSON mode, which guarantees the message the model generates is in JSON. When using JSON mode you MUST also instruct the model to produce JSON yourself with a system or a user message.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

<OperationTitleSection slot="title">

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>PATCH</b></Pill> /v1/agents/\{agent\_id\}/version \{#operation-agents_api_v1_agents_update_version\}

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_Update an agent version._

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

Switch the version of an agent.

</OperationDescriptionSection>

<OperationCodeSamplesSection slot="code-samples">

<TabbedSection>

<SectionTab

  tags={{"codeSample":"python"}}
>

Python

</SectionTab>

<SectionContent
  slot="content"
  id="operation-agents_api_v1_agents_update_version+code-samples+python"
>

<CodeSample>

```python
from mistralai import Mistral
import os


with Mistral(
    api_key=os.getenv("MISTRAL_API_KEY", ""),
) as mistral:

    res = mistral.beta.agents.update_version(agent_id="<id>", version=157995)

    # Handle response
    print(res)


```

</CodeSample>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### type \{#operation-agents_api_v1_agents_update_version+responses+200+application-json+completion_args+completionargs+response_format+responseformat+type\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

An object specifying the format that the model must output. Setting to `\{ "type": "json_object" \}` enables JSON mode, which guarantees the message the model generates is in JSON. When using JSON mode you MUST also instruct the model to produce JSON yourself with a system or a user message.
